  You are tasked with scanning and indexing the jobswipe codebase to build context for an upcoming audit. This is a
  preparatory task - do NOT make any code changes.

  Your goal is to systematically explore the project structure and provide a comprehensive summary of the
  architecture.

  Please perform the following steps:

      1. Root-level exploration: Read and analyze these key files:


          * README.md (project overview)

          * requirements.txt (Python dependencies)

          * docker-compose.yml and docker-compose.production.yml (containerization)

          * fly.toml (deployment config)

          * main.py (entry point)
      2. Backend architecture exploration: Explore the backend/ directory structure:


          * Read backend/README.md

          * Read backend/requirements.txt

          * Explore backend/api/ - understand the API structure (routers, middleware)

          * Explore backend/services/ - understand the service layer

          * Explore backend/db/ - understand database models and configuration

          * Explore backend/workers/ - understand background workers and tasks

          * Review backend/docs/ADR-*.md files to understand architectural decisions
      3. Frontend exploration: Explore the flutter/ directory:


          * Read flutter/pubspec.yaml to understand dependencies

          * Explore the main app structure
      4. Infrastructure and deployment: Review:


          * backup/ directory scripts

          * Dockerfile configurations

          * Procfile
      5. Testing structure: Review the test files to understand testing approach

  After completing your exploration, provide a comprehensive summary that includes:

      * Project overview and purpose
      * Technology stack (backend, frontend, database, deployment)
      * Key architectural components and their responsibilities
      * API endpoints structure
      * Database models overview
      * Background job processing system
      * Security considerations (auth, middleware)
      * Deployment infrastructure
      * Any notable patterns or architectural decisions

  Use the attempt_completion tool to deliver your final summary. This summary will serve as the "memory bank" for the
  upcoming audit.

  IMPORTANT: These instructions supersede any general instructions for the ask mode. Only perform exploration and
  analysis - do NOT make any code changes.

   # JobSwipe Codebase Architecture Summary

   ## Project Overview

   JobSwipe is a production-ready job search application with a Tinder-like swipe interface, powered by AI matching
   and automation. The system consists of a comprehensive FastAPI backend, a Flutter-based cross-platform mobile
   app, and a full infrastructure stack deployed on Fly.io.

   Readiness Score: ~70%

       * Backend: Fully implemented with 15+ services and comprehensive API
       * Mobile App: Basic Flutter structure created; implementation in progress
       * Infrastructure: Production deployment on Fly.io with monitoring
       * Security: Comprehensive security measures and API key management

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Technology Stack

   ### Backend

       * Framework: FastAPI 0.109.1+ (Python 3.12)
       * Database: PostgreSQL 15 with SQLAlchemy 2.0.23+ ORM
       * Migrations: Alembic 1.13.1+
       * Cache/Message Broker: Redis 7-alpine, RabbitMQ 3-management
       * Task Queue: Celery 5.3.6+
       * AI/ML:
           * Ollama (self-hosted LLM for embeddings)

           * Sentence Transformers (all-MiniLM-L6-v2 model)

           * OpenAI integration (optional)
       * Storage: MinIO/S3 compatible
       * Monitoring: Prometheus, Grafana, Jaeger (OpenTelemetry)
       * Security:
           * JWT authentication with python-jose

           * Passlib with bcrypt/argon2

           * Fernet encryption for PII

           * FastAPI-limiter for rate limiting

   ### Frontend (Mobile App)

       * Framework: Flutter 3.x (Dart SDK >=3.0.0 <4.0.0)
       * State Management: BLoC pattern (flutter_bloc 8.1.3+)
       * Dependency Injection: get_it 7.6.4+
       * Networking: Dio 5.4.0+ with retry logic
       * Local Storage:
           * Hive 2.2.3+ (NoSQL)

           * SQLite 2.3.0+

           * Flutter Secure Storage 9.0.0+
       * Firebase: Core, Messaging, Analytics, Crashlytics
       * UI: Material Design with custom swipe interface (flutter_card_swiper 7.0.0+)
       * Biometrics: local_auth 2.1.8+

   ### Deployment Infrastructure

       * Platform: Fly.io (cloud platform)
       * Containerization: Docker with multi-stage builds
       * Orchestration: Docker Compose (dev), Fly.io (production)
       * Auto-scaling: CPU/memory-based with configurable limits
       * Monitoring Stack:
           * Prometheus (metrics collection)

           * Grafana (dashboards)

           * Jaeger (distributed tracing)

           * OpenSearch (search and analytics)
       * Backup: AWS S3 with encrypted backups

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Key Architectural Components

   ### 1. API Layer (backend/api/ (backend/api/))

   Main Entry Point: backend/api/main.py (backend/api/main.py:1)

   Routers (9 total):

       * auth.py (backend/api/routers/auth.py:1) - Authentication, registration, MFA, OAuth2
       * jobs.py (backend/api/routers/jobs.py:1) - Job feed, matching, swipe actions
       * applications.py (backend/api/routers/applications.py:1) - Application tasks, status tracking
       * profile.py (backend/api/routers/profile.py:1) - User profile management
       * analytics.py (backend/api/routers/analytics.py:1) - Analytics and reporting
       * notifications.py (backend/api/routers/notifications.py:1) - Push/email notifications
       * application_automation.py (backend/api/routers/application_automation.py:1) - Automation endpoints
       * job_deduplication.py (backend/api/routers/job_deduplication.py:1) - Job deduplication
       * job_categorization.py (backend/api/routers/job_categorization.py:1) - Job categorization
       * jobs_ingestion.py (backend/api/routers/jobs_ingestion.py:1) - Job ingestion from external sources
       * api_keys.py (backend/api/routers/api_keys.py:1) - API key management

   Middleware Stack:

       * api_key_auth.py (backend/api/middleware/api_key_auth.py:1) - API key validation for internal services
       * input_sanitization.py (backend/api/middleware/input_sanitization.py:1) - XSS prevention, HTML encoding
       * output_encoding.py (backend/api/middleware/output_encoding.py:1) - Response encoding
       * compression.py (backend/api/middleware/compression.py:1) - Brotli compression
       * file_validation.py (backend/api/middleware/file_validation.py:1) - File upload validation
       * error_handling.py (backend/api/middleware/error_handling.py:1) - Centralized error handling
       * request_deduplication.py (backend/api/middleware/request_deduplication.py:1) - Duplicate request prevention

   Validators: validators.py (backend/api/validators.py:1) - Pydantic-based input validation

   ### 2. Service Layer (backend/services/ (backend/services/))

   15+ Services:

       * matching.py (backend/services/matching.py:1) - Hybrid BM25 + embeddings + rule-based job matching
       * application_service.py (backend/services/application_service.py:1) - Application task management
       * embedding_service.py (backend/services/embedding_service.py:1) - Sentence Transformers embeddings with
   Redis caching
       * job_ingestion_service.py (backend/services/job_ingestion_service.py:1) - Job ingestion from RSS,
   Greenhouse, Lever
       * job_deduplication.py (backend/services/job_deduplication.py:1) - Fuzzy deduplication (simhash)
       * job_categorization.py (backend/services/job_categorization.py:1) - spaCy-based categorization
       * notification_service.py (backend/services/notification_service.py:1) - Push/email notifications
       * push_notification_service.py (backend/services/push_notification_service.py:1) - APNs/FCM integration
       * oauth2_service.py (backend/services/oauth2_service.py:1) - Google/LinkedIn OAuth2
       * mfa_service.py (backend/services/mfa_service.py:1) - TOTP + backup codes
       * api_key_service.py (backend/services/api_key_service.py:1) - API key management
       * analytics_service.py (backend/services/analytics_service.py:1) - Analytics and reporting
       * application_automation.py (backend/services/application_automation.py:1) - Playwright-based automation
       * resume_parser.py (backend/services/resume_parser.py:1) - PDF/DOCX resume parsing
       * resume_parser_enhanced.py (backend/services/resume_parser_enhanced.py:1) - Enhanced resume parsing
       * cover_letter_service.py (backend/services/cover_letter_service.py:1) - Cover letter generation
       * storage.py (backend/services/storage.py:1) - MinIO/S3 file storage
       * captcha_detector.py (backend/services/captcha_detector.py:1) - CAPTCHA detection
       * domain_service.py (backend/services/domain_service.py:1) - ATS type detection
       * ab_testing.py (backend/services/ab_testing.py:1) - A/B testing framework

   ### 3. Data Layer (backend/db/ (backend/db/))

   Database Configuration: database.py (backend/db/database.py:1)

       * SQLAlchemy 2.0.23+ with connection pooling
       * Pool size: 20, max overflow: 30
       * Alembic migrations for schema versioning

   Models (10 core models in models.py (backend/db/models.py:1)):

       * User (backend/db/models.py:43) - User accounts with MFA, lockout, email verification
       * CandidateProfile (backend/db/models.py:76) - User profiles with encrypted PII (full_name, phone)
       * Job (backend/db/models.py:115) - Job listings with source tracking
       * JobIndex (backend/db/models.py:141) - Search index with embeddings
       * UserJobInteraction (backend/db/models.py:156) - Swipe actions and interactions
       * ApplicationTask (backend/db/models.py:176) - Application automation tasks
       * ApplicationAuditLog (backend/db/models.py:198) - Detailed audit trail
       * Notification (backend/db/models.py:248) - User notifications
       * UserNotificationPreferences (backend/db/models.py:273) - Notification preferences
       * DeviceToken (backend/db/models.py:314) - Push notification tokens
       * NotificationTemplate (backend/db/models.py:337) - Customizable notification templates
       * ApiKey (backend/db/models.py:358) - Internal service API keys
       * ApiKeyUsageLog (backend/db/models.py:390) - API key usage auditing
       * Domain (backend/db/models.py:217) - ATS type detection and rate limiting
       * CoverLetterTemplate (backend/db/models.py:231) - Cover letter templates
       * FailedLoginAttempt (backend/db/models.py:98) - Security tracking

   Encryption: EncryptedString (backend/db/models.py:24) type decorator for PII fields using Fernet

   ### 4. Background Workers (backend/workers/ (backend/workers/))

   Celery Configuration: celery_app.py (backend/workers/celery_app.py:1)

       * Redis broker and result backend
       * Task queues: notifications, ingestion, analytics, cleanup
       * Beat schedule for periodic tasks (daily cleanup, hourly embeddings)

   Workers:

       * app_agent_worker.py (backend/workers/app_agent_worker.py:1) - Application automation worker
       * embedding_worker.py (backend/workers/embedding_worker.py:1) - Embedding generation worker

   Task Modules:

       * celery_tasks/notification_tasks.py (backend/workers/celery_tasks/notification_tasks.py:1) - Notification
   delivery
       * celery_tasks/ingestion_tasks.py (backend/workers/celery_tasks/ingestion_tasks.py:1) - Job ingestion
       * celery_tasks/analytics_tasks.py (backend/workers/celery_tasks/analytics_tasks.py:1) - Analytics snapshots
       * celery_tasks/cleanup_tasks.py (backend/workers/celery_tasks/cleanup_tasks.py:1) - Token/session cleanup

   Application Agents:

       * agents/greenhouse.py (backend/workers/application_agent/agents/greenhouse.py:1) - Greenhouse ATS automation
       * agents/lever.py (backend/workers/application_agent/agents/lever.py:1) - Lever ATS automation

   Ingestion Sources:

       * ingestion/greenhouse.py (backend/workers/ingestion/greenhouse.py:1) - Greenhouse API integration
       * ingestion/lever.py (backend/workers/ingestion/lever.py:1) - Lever API integration
       * ingestion/rss.py (backend/workers/ingestion/rss.py:1) - RSS feed parsing

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## API Endpoints Structure

   ### Authentication (/api/v1/auth (backend/api/routers/auth.py:1))

       * POST /register - User registration with password validation
       * POST /login - Login with rate limiting and account lockout
       * POST /refresh - Token refresh
       * GET /me - Current user info
       * POST /mfa/setup - MFA setup
       * POST /oauth2/google - Google OAuth2
       * POST /oauth2/linkedin - LinkedIn OAuth2

   ### Jobs (/api/v1/jobs (backend/api/routers/jobs.py:1))

       * GET /matches - Get matched jobs with scoring (BM25 + embeddings)
       * GET /feed - Personalized job feed with cursor pagination
       * GET /{job_id} - Job details
       * POST /{job_id}/swipe - Record swipe action (right/left)

   ### Applications (/api/v1/applications (backend/api/routers/applications.py:1))

       * POST / - Create application task
       * GET / - List user applications
       * GET /{job_id}/status - Application status
       * GET /{job_id}/audit - Application audit log
       * POST /{job_id}/cancel - Cancel application

   ### Profile (/api/v1/profile (backend/api/routers/profile.py:1))

       * GET / - Get user profile
       * PUT / - Update profile
       * POST /resume - Upload resume
       * GET /analytics - Profile analytics

   ### Analytics (/api/v1/analytics (backend/api/routers/analytics.py:1))

       * GET /matching - Matching performance metrics
       * GET /applications - Application analytics
       * GET /user-behavior - User behavior insights

   ### Notifications (/api/v1/notifications (backend/api/routers/notifications.py:1))

       * GET / - List notifications
       * POST /{id}/read - Mark as read
       * POST /preferences - Update notification preferences

   ### Ingestion (Admin) (/api/v1/ingestion (backend/api/routers/jobs_ingestion.py:1))

       * POST /sources/greenhouse/sync - Sync Greenhouse jobs
       * POST /sources/lever/sync - Sync Lever jobs
       * POST /sources/rss/sync - Sync RSS feeds
       * POST /deduplicate/run - Run deduplication
       * POST /categorize/run - Run categorization

   ### API Keys (/api/v1/api_keys (backend/api/routers/api_keys.py:1))

       * POST / - Create API key
       * GET / - List API keys
       * DELETE /{id} - Revoke API key

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Database Models Overview

   ### Core Entities

       1. User - Authentication, MFA, lockout, email verification
       2. CandidateProfile - User profile with encrypted PII (full_name, phone)
       3. Job - Job listings with source tracking (Greenhouse, Lever, RSS)
       4. JobIndex - Search index with embeddings and facets
       5. UserJobInteraction - Swipe actions and user feedback
       6. ApplicationTask - Application automation tasks with status tracking
       7. ApplicationAuditLog - Detailed audit trail for transparency
       8. Notification - User notifications (push/email)
       9. UserNotificationPreferences - Granular notification preferences
       10. DeviceToken - Push notification tokens (APNs/FCM)
       11. ApiKey - Internal service API keys with permissions
       12. ApiKeyUsageLog - API key usage auditing
       13. Domain - ATS type detection and rate limiting policies
       14. CoverLetterTemplate - Customizable cover letter templates
       15. FailedLoginAttempt - Security tracking for lockout

   ### Key Relationships

       * User â†’ CandidateProfile (1:1)
       * User â†’ UserJobInteraction (1:N)
       * User â†’ ApplicationTask (1:N)
       * User â†’ Notification (1:N)
       * User â†’ DeviceToken (1:N)
       * User â†’ ApiKey (1:N as creator)
       * Job â†’ UserJobInteraction (1:N)
       * Job â†’ ApplicationTask (1:N)
       * Job â†’ JobIndex (1:1)
       * ApplicationTask â†’ ApplicationAuditLog (1:N)
       * ApplicationTask â†’ Notification (1:N)

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Background Job Processing System

   ### Celery Architecture

       * Broker: Redis (message queue)
       * Result Backend: Redis (task results)
       * Task Queues: notifications, ingestion, analytics, cleanup
       * Worker Concurrency: 4 workers per instance
       * Task Time Limits: 30 minutes hard, 25 minutes soft

   ### Periodic Tasks (Beat Schedule)

       * Daily at 2 AM UTC: Cleanup expired tokens
       * Daily at 3 AM UTC: Cleanup old sessions
       * Daily at 8 AM UTC: Send daily digest emails
       * Hourly: Refresh job embeddings
       * Hourly at 5 minutes past: Generate analytics snapshots

   ### Application Automation

       * Playwright-based browser automation
       * ATS Support: Greenhouse, Lever
       * CAPTCHA Detection: Human-in-the-loop system
       * Audit Logging: Step-by-step audit trail
       * Retry Logic: Exponential backoff with max 5 retries

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Security Considerations

   ### Authentication

       * JWT Tokens: Access tokens (60 min), Refresh tokens (7 days)
       * Password Hashing: Argon2 with PBKDF2 fallback
       * MFA: TOTP + backup codes
       * OAuth2: Google, LinkedIn integration
       * Account Lockout: Exponential backoff after 5 failed attempts

   ### Authorization

       * Role-based: user, admin roles
       * API Keys: Scoped permissions for internal services
       * Rate Limiting: Redis-backed with per-endpoint limits
       * Request Deduplication: Prevent duplicate submissions

   ### Data Protection

       * PII Encryption: Fernet encryption for full_name, phone
       * Input Sanitization: XSS prevention, HTML encoding
       * Output Encoding: Secure response encoding
       * File Validation: MIME type and size validation
       * CORS: Configured for mobile app origins

   ### Security Headers

       * CSP (Content Security Policy)
       * HSTS (HTTP Strict Transport Security)
       * X-Frame-Options
       * X-Content-Type-Options

   ### Audit Logging

       * Security Logger: Separate security event logging
       * Failed Login Tracking: IP, user agent, timestamp
       * API Key Usage: Endpoint, method, status, duration
       * Application Audit: Step-by-step automation audit

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Deployment Infrastructure

   ### Fly.io Configuration (fly.toml (fly.toml:1))

       * App: jobswipe-9obhra
       * Region: iad (primary)
       * Auto-scaling:
           * Min machines: 2

           * Max machines: 10

           * Scale based on CPU (70% threshold), memory (80% threshold), request queue
       * Health Checks: /health endpoint every 15s
       * Metrics: /metrics endpoint on port 9091

   ### Docker Configuration (Dockerfile (Dockerfile:1))

       * Multi-stage build: Python 3.12-slim-bullseye
       * Non-root user: appuser (UID 1000)
       * Health check: curl to /health endpoint
       * Port: 8080
       * Command: uvicorn backend.api.main:app

   ### Docker Compose Services

       * postgres: PostgreSQL 15 with health checks
       * redis: Redis 7-alpine for caching and Celery
       * rabbitmq: RabbitMQ 3-management for Celery broker
       * backend: FastAPI API server
       * celery-worker: Application automation worker
       * celery-flower: Celery monitoring UI
       * opensearch: Search and analytics
       * opensearch-dashboards: Visualization
       * prometheus: Metrics collection
       * grafana: Dashboards
       * jaeger: Distributed tracing
       * vault: HashiCorp Vault for secrets
       * ollama: Self-hosted LLM for embeddings

   ### Backup & Disaster Recovery

       * Backup Script: backup/backup_postgres.sh (backup/backup_postgres.sh:1)
           * Daily encrypted backups to AWS S3

           * AES-256-CBC encryption with PBKDF2

           * Retention: 7 days
       * Restore Script: backup/restore_postgres.sh (backup/restore_postgres.sh:1)
       * Disaster Recovery Runbook: backup/DISASTER_RECOVERY_RUNBOOK.md (backup/DISASTER_RECOVERY_RUNBOOK.md:1)
           * RTO: Database 2-4 hours, Service 30 min-2 hours

           * RPO: Database 24 hours (daily backups)

           * Testing: Monthly backup testing, quarterly failover

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Notable Patterns & Architectural Decisions

   ### ADRs (Architecture Decision Records)

       1. ADR-001: Choose FastAPI as Web Framework (ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md 
   (backend/docs/adr/ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md:1))
           * Performance, type safety, async support, automatic documentation
       2. ADR-002: Choose PostgreSQL as Primary Database (ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md 
   (backend/docs/adr/ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md:1))
           * ACID compliance, JSON support, full-text search, extensions
       3. ADR-003: Use JWT for API Authentication (ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md 
   (backend/docs/adr/ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md:1))
           * Stateless, scalable, mobile-friendly

   ### Design Patterns

       * Service Layer Pattern: Business logic separated from API layer
       * Repository Pattern: Data access abstraction via SQLAlchemy ORM
       * Middleware Pattern: Cross-cutting concerns (auth, validation, compression)
       * Observer Pattern: Notification system with multiple channels
       * Strategy Pattern: ATS-specific automation agents
       * Factory Pattern: Worker task creation
       * Decorator Pattern: Encryption type decorator for PII fields

   ### Key Features

       * Hybrid Matching: BM25 (50%) + Embeddings (30%) + Rule-based (20%)
       * Caching: Redis for job feeds, embeddings, rate limiting
       * Distributed Tracing: OpenTelemetry with Jaeger
       * Metrics: Prometheus with custom metrics (matching duration, score distribution)
       * Graceful Degradation: Fallback when external services unavailable
       * Audit Trail: Comprehensive logging for compliance and debugging

 â”‚ ğŸ’­ Reasoning                                                                                                    â”‚

 â”‚ I see that in orchestrator mode, I cannot use read_file directly. I need to delegate this task to a mode that   â”‚
 â”‚ can read files. Let me use the new_task tool to delegate this exploration task to an appropriate mode.          â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ Since I need to scan and understand the codebase, I should delegate this to "Ask" mode which is designed for    â”‚
 â”‚ understanding and analyzing code without making changes.                                                        â”‚
 â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

 â”‚ # JobSwipe Codebase Architecture Summary                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Project Overview                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ JobSwipe is a production-ready job search application with a Tinder-like swipe interface, powered by AI         â”‚
 â”‚ matching and automation. The system consists of a comprehensive FastAPI backend, a Flutter-based cross-platform â”‚
 â”‚  mobile app, and a full infrastructure stack deployed on Fly.io.                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ Readiness Score: ~70%                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Backend: Fully implemented with 15+ services and comprehensive API                                        â”‚
 â”‚     * Mobile App: Basic Flutter structure created; implementation in progress                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Infrastructure: Production deployment on Fly.io with monitoring                                           â”‚
 â”‚     * Security: Comprehensive security measures and API key management                                          â”‚

 â”‚         * JWT authentication with python-jose                                                                   â”‚

 â”‚ ## Database Models Overview                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Core Entities                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     1. User - Authentication, MFA, lockout, email verification                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     2. CandidateProfile - User profile with encrypted PII (full_name, phone)                                    â”‚
 â”‚     3. Job - Job listings with source tracking (Greenhouse, Lever, RSS)                                         â”‚
 â”‚     4. JobIndex - Search index with embeddings and facets                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     5. UserJobInteraction - Swipe actions and user feedback                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     6. ApplicationTask - Application automation tasks with status tracking                                      â”‚
 â”‚     7. ApplicationAuditLog - Detailed audit trail for transparency                                              â”‚
 â”‚     8. Notification - User notifications (push/email)                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     9. UserNotificationPreferences - Granular notification preferences                                          â”‚
 â”‚     10. DeviceToken - Push notification tokens (APNs/FCM)                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     11. ApiKey - Internal service API keys with permissions                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     12. ApiKeyUsageLog - API key usage auditing                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     13. Domain - ATS type detection and rate limiting policies                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     14. CoverLetterTemplate - Customizable cover letter templates                                               â”‚
 â”‚     15. FailedLoginAttempt - Security tracking for lockout                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Key Relationships                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ CandidateProfile (1:1)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ UserJobInteraction (1:N)                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ ApplicationTask (1:N)                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ Notification (1:N)                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ DeviceToken (1:N)                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ ApiKey (1:N as creator)                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Job â†’ UserJobInteraction (1:N)                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Job â†’ ApplicationTask (1:N)                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Job â†’ JobIndex (1:1)                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * ApplicationTask â†’ ApplicationAuditLog (1:N)                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * ApplicationTask â†’ Notification (1:N)                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- â”‚
 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Background Job Processing System                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Celery Architecture                                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Broker: Redis (message queue)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * Result Backend: Redis (task results)                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Task Queues: notifications, ingestion, analytics, cleanup                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Worker Concurrency: 4 workers per instance                                                                â”‚
 â”‚     * Task Time Limits: 30 minutes hard, 25 minutes soft                                                        â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Periodic Tasks (Beat Schedule)                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 2 AM UTC: Cleanup expired tokens                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 3 AM UTC: Cleanup old sessions                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 8 AM UTC: Send daily digest emails                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Hourly: Refresh job embeddings                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Hourly at 5 minutes past: Generate analytics snapshots                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Application Automation                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Playwright-based browser automation                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     * ATS Support: Greenhouse, Lever                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * CAPTCHA Detection: Human-in-the-loop system                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Audit Logging: Step-by-step audit trail                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Retry Logic: Exponential backoff with max 5 retries                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- â”‚
 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Security Considerations                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Authentication                                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * JWT Tokens: Access tokens (60 min), Refresh tokens (7 days)                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Password Hashing: Argon2 with PBKDF2 fallback                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * MFA: TOTP + backup codes                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     * OAuth2: Google, LinkedIn integration                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Account Lockout: Exponential backoff after 5 failed attempts                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Authorization                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Role-based: user, admin roles                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * API Keys: Scoped permissions for internal services                                                        â”‚
 â”‚     * Rate Limiting: Redis-backed with per-endpoint limits                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Request Deduplication: Prevent duplicate submissions                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Data Protection                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * PII Encryption: Fernet encryption for full_name, phone                                                    â”‚
 â”‚     * Input Sanitization: XSS prevention, HTML encoding                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Output Encoding: Secure response encoding                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * File Validation: MIME type and size validation                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * CORS: Configured for mobile app origins                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Security Headers                                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * CSP (Content Security Policy)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * HSTS (HTTP Strict Transport Security)                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * X-Frame-Options                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     * X-Content-Type-Options                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Audit Logging                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Security Logger: Separate security event logging                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * Failed Login Tracking: IP, user agent, timestamp                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * API Key Usage: Endpoint, method, status, duration                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Application Audit: Step-by-step automation audit                                                          â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- â”‚
 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Deployment Infrastructure                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Fly.io Configuration (fly.toml (fly.toml:1))                                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * App: jobswipe-9obhra                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Region: iad (primary)                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Auto-scaling:                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚         * Min machines: 2                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Max machines: 10                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Scale based on CPU (70% threshold), memory (80% threshold), request queue                             â”‚
 â”‚     * Health Checks: /health endpoint every 15s                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Metrics: /metrics endpoint on port 9091                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚

 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Multi-stage build: Python 3.12-slim-bullseye                                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * Non-root user: appuser (UID 1000)                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Health check: curl to /health endpoint                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚     * Port: 8080                                                                                                â”‚
 â”‚     * Command: uvicorn backend.api.main:app                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Docker Compose Services                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * postgres: PostgreSQL 15 with health checks                                                                â”‚
 â”‚     * redis: Redis 7-alpine for caching and Celery                                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * rabbitmq: RabbitMQ 3-management for Celery broker                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * backend: FastAPI API server                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * celery-worker: Application automation worker                                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * celery-flower: Celery monitoring UI                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     * opensearch: Search and analytics                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * opensearch-dashboards: Visualization                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * prometheus: Metrics collection                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * grafana: Dashboards                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     * jaeger: Distributed tracing                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * vault: HashiCorp Vault for secrets                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚     * ollama: Self-hosted LLM for embeddings                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Backup & Disaster Recovery                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Backup Script: backup/backup_postgres.sh (backup/backup_postgres.sh:1)                                    â”‚
 â”‚         * Daily encrypted backups to AWS S3                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * AES-256-CBC encryption with PBKDF2                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Retention: 7 days                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Restore Script: backup/restore_postgres.sh (backup/restore_postgres.sh:1)                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Disaster Recovery Runbook: backup/DISASTER_RECOVERY_RUNBOOK.md (backup/DISASTER_RECOVERY_RUNBOOK.md:1)    â”‚
 â”‚         * RTO: Database 2-4 hours, Service 30 min-2 hours                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * RPO: Database 24 hours (daily backups)                                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Testing: Monthly backup testing, quarterly failover                                                   â”‚

 â”‚ ## Notable Patterns & Architectural Decisions                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### ADRs (Architecture Decision Records)                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     1. ADR-001: Choose FastAPI as Web Framework (ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md                                      â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md:1))                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Performance, type safety, async support, automatic documentation                                      â”‚
 â”‚     2. ADR-002: Choose PostgreSQL as Primary Database (ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md                             â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md:1))                                                              â”‚
 â”‚         * ACID compliance, JSON support, full-text search, extensions                                           â”‚
 â”‚     3. ADR-003: Use JWT for API Authentication (ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md                                   â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md:1))                                                             â”‚
 â”‚         * Stateless, scalable, mobile-friendly                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Design Patterns                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Service Layer Pattern: Business logic separated from API layer                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Repository Pattern: Data access abstraction via SQLAlchemy ORM                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Middleware Pattern: Cross-cutting concerns (auth, validation, compression)                                â”‚
 â”‚     * Observer Pattern: Notification system with multiple channels                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * Strategy Pattern: ATS-specific automation agents                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * Factory Pattern: Worker task creation                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Decorator Pattern: Encryption type decorator for PII fields                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Key Features                                                                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Hybrid Matching: BM25 (50%) + Embeddings (30%) + Rule-based (20%)                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Caching: Redis for job feeds, embeddings, rate limiting                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Distributed Tracing: OpenTelemetry with Jaeger                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Metrics: Prometheus with custom metrics (matching duration, score distribution)                           â”‚
 â”‚     * Graceful Degradation: Fallback when external services unavailable                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Audit Trail: Comprehensive logging for compliance and debugging                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚

 âœ“ Task Completed

   Memory bank initialized. The JobSwipe codebase has been scanned and indexed.

   ## Project Overview

   JobSwipe is a production-ready job search application with a Tinder-like swipe interface, powered by AI matching
   and automation. The system consists of a comprehensive FastAPI backend, a Flutter-based cross-platform mobile
   app, and a full infrastructure stack deployed on Fly.io.

   ## Technology Stack Summary

       * Backend: FastAPI 0.109.1+, PostgreSQL 15, SQLAlchemy 2.0.23+, Redis, RabbitMQ, Celery
       * AI/ML: Ollama (self-hosted LLM), Sentence Transformers, OpenAI integration
       * Frontend: Flutter 3.x with BLoC pattern, Dio networking, Hive/SQLite storage
       * Deployment: Fly.io with Docker, Prometheus/Grafana monitoring, Jaeger tracing
       * Security: JWT auth, MFA, API keys, PII encryption, rate limiting

   ## Key Architecture Components

       1. API Layer (backend/api/ (backend/api/)): 11 routers (auth, jobs, applications, profile, analytics,
   notifications, etc.) with 7 middleware components
       2. Service Layer (backend/services/ (backend/services/)): 15+ services including matching, embeddings, job
   ingestion, deduplication, categorization, notifications, OAuth2, MFA, automation
       3. Data Layer (backend/db/ (backend/db/)): 15 core models with SQLAlchemy ORM, Alembic migrations, Fernet
   encryption for PII
       4. Background Workers (backend/workers/ (backend/workers/)): Celery with Redis broker, 4 task queues,
   periodic tasks, Playwright-based automation agents

   ## Database Models

   User, CandidateProfile, Job, JobIndex, UserJobInteraction, ApplicationTask, ApplicationAuditLog, Notification,
   UserNotificationPreferences, DeviceToken, NotificationTemplate, ApiKey, ApiKeyUsageLog, Domain,
   CoverLetterTemplate, FailedLoginAttempt

   ## Security Features

       * JWT tokens (60min access, 7day refresh)
       * Argon2 password hashing with PBKDF2 fallback
       * TOTP MFA + backup codes
       * OAuth2 (Google, LinkedIn)
       * Account lockout with exponential backoff
       * PII encryption (Fernet)
       * Input sanitization and output encoding
       * API key management with scoped permissions
       * Comprehensive audit logging

   ## Deployment Infrastructure

       * Fly.io auto-scaling (2-10 machines)
       * Docker multi-stage builds
       * 12 Docker Compose services (postgres, redis, rabbitmq, backend, celery-worker, opensearch, prometheus,
   grafana, jaeger, vault, ollama)
       * Daily encrypted backups to AWS S3
       * Disaster recovery runbook (RTO: 2-4h database, RPO: 24h)

   ## Project Status

       * Backend: âœ… Production Ready (~100%)
       * Mobile App: ğŸ”„ In Development (~30%)
       * Overall Readiness: ~70%

   The codebase is now indexed and ready for audit.

  Execute a "Deep Deployment Audit" for the JobSwipe project (FastAPI + Celery on Fly.io). This is an analysis task -
  do NOT make any code changes.

  Based on the codebase context already established, perform a focused audit on these 4 critical areas:

  ## 1. The "Web" vs "Worker" Problem

      * Read fly.toml and check if it uses [processes] to run both the web server (uvicorn) and the worker (celery)
      * Read backend/workers/celery_app.py to understand the worker configuration
      * Determine: If [processes] is not configured, how is the worker starting? If missing, background tasks will
  fail silently.

  ## 2. Port Consistency Chain

      * Read backend/api/main.py - Check what port Uvicorn launches on (default 8000 or 8080?) and if it binds to
  0.0.0.0
      * Read Dockerfile - Check what port is EXPOSEd
      * Read fly.toml - Check what internal_port is set to
      * Verify: All three must match for the deployment to work correctly

  ## 3. Database Connection Safety

      * Read backend/db/database.py - Check how DATABASE_URL is required/used
      * Read fly.toml - Verify that DATABASE_URL is NOT hardcoded but referenced as a runtime secret
      * Determine: Is the database connection properly configured for production?

  ## 4. Python Path Issues

      * Read Dockerfile - Check the WORKDIR setting
      * Read Dockerfile - Check the CMD (likely uvicorn backend.api.main:app)
      * Verify: The uvicorn command must run from the correct parent directory so Python can resolve the imports
  (e.g., from /app not /app/backend)

  ## Deliverable Format

  Provide a "Pass/Fail" report for each of these 4 items with this structure:

      ### 1. The "Web" vs "Worker" Problem
      Status: [PASS/FAIL]
      Analysis: [Your findings]
      [If FAIL] Fix Required: [Specific code block to fix it]

      ### 2. Port Consistency Chain
      Status: [PASS/FAIL]
      Analysis: [Your findings]
      [If FAIL] Fix Required: [Specific code block to fix it]

      ### 3. Database Connection Safety
      Status: [PASS/FAIL]
      Analysis: [Your findings]
      [If FAIL] Fix Required: [Specific code block to fix it]

      ### 4. Python Path Issues
      Status: [PASS/FAIL]
      Analysis: [Your findings]
      [If FAIL] Fix Required: [Specific code block to fix it]

  IMPORTANT: These instructions supersede any general instructions for the architect mode. Only perform analysis and
  provide the audit report - do NOT make any code changes. Use the attempt_completion tool to deliver your final
  report.

 âœ“ Task Completed

   # Deep Deployment Audit Report for JobSwipe Project

   ## Executive Summary

   Overall Status: 3 PASS, 1 FAIL

   The deployment configuration has a critical issue with the Celery worker not being configured to run, which will
   cause all background tasks to fail silently.

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ### 1. The "Web" vs "Worker" Problem

   Status: FAIL

   Analysis:

       * fly.toml (fly.toml:18) contains processes = ['app'] under [http_service], which is NOT a [processes]
   section
       * There is NO [processes] section that defines multiple processes (web and worker)
       * backend/workers/celery_app.py (backend/workers/celery_app.py:81-82) has if __name__ == "__main__": 
   celery_app.start() but this will never execute in production
       * The Celery worker is configured with Redis broker/backend and has periodic tasks defined (beat_schedule)
       * Critical Issue: Without a [processes] section, the worker will never start, causing all background tasks
   (notifications, job ingestion, analytics, cleanup) to fail silently

   Fix Required:

       # Add this section to fly.toml after the [http_service] section
       [processes]
         app = "python -m uvicorn backend.api.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8080"
         worker = "celery -A backend.workers.celery_app worker --loglevel=info --concurrency=4"

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ### 2. Port Consistency Chain

   Status: PASS

   Analysis:

       * backend/api/main.py (backend/api/main.py:392): Uvicorn runs on port 8080 and binds to 0.0.0.0
       * Dockerfile (Dockerfile:47): EXPOSE 8080 - Exposes port 8080
       * Dockerfile (Dockerfile:53): CMD runs uvicorn on port 8080
       * fly.toml (fly.toml:12): internal_port = 8080 - Sets internal port to 8080
       * All three components are consistent on port 8080

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ### 3. Database Connection Safety

   Status: PASS

   Analysis:

       * backend/db/database.py (backend/db/database.py:17-19): DATABASE_URL is retrieved from environment variable
   with SQLite fallback for development
       * fly.toml (fly.toml:1-82): No hardcoded DATABASE_URL found - configuration relies on runtime secrets
       * The database connection is properly configured for production using environment variables

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ### 4. Python Path Issues

   Status: PASS

   Analysis:

       * Dockerfile (Dockerfile:28): WORKDIR /app - Sets working directory to /app
       * Dockerfile (Dockerfile:38): COPY backend/ /app/backend/ - Copies backend code to /app/backend/
       * Dockerfile (Dockerfile:53): CMD runs python -m uvicorn backend.api.main:app from /app
       * The uvicorn command runs from the correct parent directory (/app), allowing Python to resolve the import
   path backend.api.main as /app/backend/api/main.py

   -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   ---

   ## Critical Action Required

   The Celery worker MUST be configured to run. Without the [processes] section in fly.toml (fly.toml:1-82), the
   following background features will fail silently:

       * Email notifications (daily digests, application updates)
       * Job ingestion from external sources (Greenhouse, Lever, RSS)
       * Analytics snapshots and reporting
       * Token and session cleanup
       * Job embedding refresh

   This is a production-critical issue that will significantly impact application functionality.

 â”‚     * Orchestration: Docker Compose (dev), Fly.io (production)                                                  â”‚

 â”‚     * Monitoring Stack:                                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚         * Prometheus (metrics collection)                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Grafana (dashboards)                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Jaeger (distributed tracing)                                                                          â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * OpenSearch (search and analytics)                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Backup: AWS S3 with encrypted backups                                                                     â”‚

 â”‚     1. User - Authentication, MFA, lockout, email verification                                                  â”‚

 â”‚     3. Job - Job listings with source tracking (Greenhouse, Lever, RSS)                                         â”‚

 â”‚     6. ApplicationTask - Application automation tasks with status tracking                                      â”‚
 â”‚     7. ApplicationAuditLog - Detailed audit trail for transparency                                              â”‚
 â”‚     8. Notification - User notifications (push/email)                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     9. UserNotificationPreferences - Granular notification preferences                                          â”‚
 â”‚     10. DeviceToken - Push notification tokens (APNs/FCM)                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     11. ApiKey - Internal service API keys with permissions                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     12. ApiKeyUsageLog - API key usage auditing                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     13. Domain - ATS type detection and rate limiting policies                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     14. CoverLetterTemplate - Customizable cover letter templates                                               â”‚
 â”‚     15. FailedLoginAttempt - Security tracking for lockout                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Key Relationships                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ CandidateProfile (1:1)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ UserJobInteraction (1:N)                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     * User â†’ ApplicationTask (1:N)                                                                              â”‚

 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Background Job Processing System                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Celery Architecture                                                                                         â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Broker: Redis (message queue)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * Result Backend: Redis (task results)                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Task Queues: notifications, ingestion, analytics, cleanup                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Worker Concurrency: 4 workers per instance                                                                â”‚
 â”‚     * Task Time Limits: 30 minutes hard, 25 minutes soft                                                        â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Periodic Tasks (Beat Schedule)                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 2 AM UTC: Cleanup expired tokens                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 3 AM UTC: Cleanup old sessions                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Daily at 8 AM UTC: Send daily digest emails                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Hourly: Refresh job embeddings                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Hourly at 5 minutes past: Generate analytics snapshots                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Application Automation                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Playwright-based browser automation                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚     * ATS Support: Greenhouse, Lever                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * CAPTCHA Detection: Human-in-the-loop system                                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Audit Logging: Step-by-step audit trail                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Retry Logic: Exponential backoff with max 5 retries                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- â”‚
 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Security Considerations                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Authentication                                                                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * JWT Tokens: Access tokens (60 min), Refresh tokens (7 days)                                               â”‚
 â”‚     * Password Hashing: Argon2 with PBKDF2 fallback                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * MFA: TOTP + backup codes                                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚     * OAuth2: Google, LinkedIn integration                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Account Lockout: Exponential backoff after 5 failed attempts                                              â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Authorization                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Role-based: user, admin roles                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * API Keys: Scoped permissions for internal services                                                        â”‚
 â”‚     * Rate Limiting: Redis-backed with per-endpoint limits                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Request Deduplication: Prevent duplicate submissions                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Data Protection                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * PII Encryption: Fernet encryption for full_name, phone                                                    â”‚
 â”‚     * Input Sanitization: XSS prevention, HTML encoding                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Output Encoding: Secure response encoding                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * File Validation: MIME type and size validation                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * CORS: Configured for mobile app origins                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Security Headers                                                                                            â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * CSP (Content Security Policy)                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚     * HSTS (HTTP Strict Transport Security)                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * X-Frame-Options                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚     * X-Content-Type-Options                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Audit Logging                                                                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Security Logger: Separate security event logging                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * Failed Login Tracking: IP, user agent, timestamp                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * API Key Usage: Endpoint, method, status, duration                                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Application Audit: Step-by-step automation audit                                                          â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- â”‚
 â”‚ -----                                                                                                           â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ## Deployment Infrastructure                                                                                    â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Fly.io Configuration (fly.toml (fly.toml:1))                                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * App: jobswipe-9obhra                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚     * Region: iad (primary)                                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Auto-scaling:                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚         * Min machines: 2                                                                                       â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Max machines: 10                                                                                      â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Scale based on CPU (70% threshold), memory (80% threshold), request queue                             â”‚
 â”‚     * Health Checks: /health endpoint every 15s                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Metrics: /metrics endpoint on port 9091                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Docker Configuration (Dockerfile (Dockerfile:1))                                                            â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚

 â”‚ ## Notable Patterns & Architectural Decisions                                                                   â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### ADRs (Architecture Decision Records)                                                                        â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     1. ADR-001: Choose FastAPI as Web Framework (ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md                                      â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-001-choose-fastapi.md:1))                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚         * Performance, type safety, async support, automatic documentation                                      â”‚
 â”‚     2. ADR-002: Choose PostgreSQL as Primary Database (ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md                             â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-002-choose-postgresql.md:1))                                                              â”‚
 â”‚         * ACID compliance, JSON support, full-text search, extensions                                           â”‚
 â”‚     3. ADR-003: Use JWT for API Authentication (ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md                                   â”‚
 â”‚ (backend/docs/adr/ADR-003-jwt-authentication.md:1))                                                             â”‚
 â”‚         * Stateless, scalable, mobile-friendly                                                                  â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Design Patterns                                                                                             â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Service Layer Pattern: Business logic separated from API layer                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Repository Pattern: Data access abstraction via SQLAlchemy ORM                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Middleware Pattern: Cross-cutting concerns (auth, validation, compression)                                â”‚
 â”‚     * Observer Pattern: Notification system with multiple channels                                              â”‚
 â”‚     * Strategy Pattern: ATS-specific automation agents                                                          â”‚
 â”‚     * Factory Pattern: Worker task creation                                                                     â”‚
 â”‚     * Decorator Pattern: Encryption type decorator for PII fields                                               â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚ ### Key Features                                                                                                â”‚
 â”‚                                                                                                                 â”‚
 â”‚     * Hybrid Matching: BM25 (50%) + Embeddings (30%) + Rule-based (20%)                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Caching: Redis for job feeds, embeddings, rate limiting                                                   â”‚
 â”‚     * Distributed Tracing: OpenTelemetry with Jaeger                                                            â”‚
 â”‚     * Metrics: Prometheus with custom metrics (matching duration, score distribution)                           â”‚
 â”‚     * Graceful Degradation: Fallback when external services unavailable                                         â”‚
 â”‚     * Audit Trail: Comprehensive logging for compliance and debugging                                           â”‚

 âœ“ Task Completed

   Memory bank initialized. The JobSwipe codebase has been scanned and indexed.

   ## Project Overview

   JobSwipe is a production-ready job search application with a Tinder-like swipe interface, powered by AI matching
   and automation. The system consists of a comprehensive FastAPI backend, a Flutter-based cross-platform mobile app,
   and a full infrastructure stack deployed on Fly.io.

   ## Technology Stack Summary

       * Backend: FastAPI 0.109.1+, PostgreSQL 15, SQLAlchemy 2.0.23+, Redis, RabbitMQ, Celery
       * AI/ML: Ollama (self-hosted LLM), Sentence Transformers, OpenAI integration
       * Frontend: Flutter 3.x with BLoC pattern, Dio networking, Hive/SQLite storage
       * Deployment: Fly.io with Docker, Prometheus/Grafana monitoring, Jaeger tracing
       * Security: JWT auth, MFA, API keys, PII encryption, rate limiting

   ## Key Architecture Components

       1. API Layer (backend/api/ (backend/api/)): 11 routers (auth, jobs, applications, profile, analytics,
   notifications, etc.) with 7 middleware components
       2. Service Layer (backend/services/ (backend/services/)): 15+ services including matching, embeddings, job
   ingestion, deduplication, categorization, notifications, OAuth2, MFA, automation
       3. Data Layer (backend/db/ (backend/db/)): 15 core models with SQLAlchemy ORM, Alembic migrations, Fernet
   encryption for PII
       4. Background Workers (backend/workers/ (backend/workers/)): Celery with Redis broker, 4 task queues, periodic
   tasks, Playwright-based automation agents

   ## Database Models

   User, CandidateProfile, Job, JobIndex, UserJobInteraction, ApplicationTask, ApplicationAuditLog, Notification,
   UserNotificationPreferences, DeviceToken, NotificationTemplate, ApiKey, ApiKeyUsageLog, Domain,
   CoverLetterTemplate, FailedLoginAttempt

   ## Security Features

       * JWT tokens (60min access, 7day refresh)
       * Argon2 password hashing with PBKDF2 fallback
       * TOTP MFA + backup codes
       * OAuth2 (Google, LinkedIn)
       * Account lockout with exponential backoff
       * PII encryption (Fernet)
       * Input sanitization and output encoding
       * API key management with scoped permissions
       * Comprehensive audit logging

   ## Deployment Infrastructure

       * Fly.io auto-scaling (2-10 machines)
       * Docker multi-stage builds
       * 12 Docker Compose services (postgres, redis, rabbitmq, backend, celery-worker, opensearch, prometheus,
   grafana, jaeger, vault, ollama)
       * Daily encrypted backups to AWS S3
       * Disaster recovery runbook (RTO: 2-4h database, RPO: 24h)

   ## Project Status

       * Backend: âœ… Production Ready (~100%)
       * Mobile App: ğŸ”„ In Development (~30%)
       * Overall Readiness: ~70%

   The codebase is now indexed and ready for audit.
